```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Student Association Organizational Constitution

99.03.19 Amendments approved during by the 1st Joint Class Representative Meeting of the 98 academic year

100.03.13 Amendments approved during the 1st Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 99 academic year, subject to verification.

102.11.21 3rd amendment during the 8th Cadre Meeting of the 22nd academic year of 102.

105.12.17 Amendments approved during the 12th Cadre Meeting of the 25th academic year of 105.

107.11.14 Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 4th academic year of 107, subject to verification.

109.04.09 Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 8th academic year of 108, subject to verification.

109.07.02 Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 10th academic year of 108, subject to verification.

110.07.01 Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 10th academic year of 109, subject to verification.

111.04.06 Amendments approved during the 3rd Regular Meeting of the 29th Student Council Assembly.

111.09.06 Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 1st academic year of 111, for reference.

111.11.30 Amendments made during the 5th Extraordinary Meeting of the 30th Student Council Assembly.

112.02.21 Amendments made during the 2nd Regular Meeting of the 30th Student Council Assembly.

112.05.04 Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 12th academic year of 111, for reference.

112.07.28 Amendments made during the 1th Extraordinary Meeting of the 31th Student Council Assembly..

113.10.15 Amendments made during the 2nd Regular Meeting of the 32th Student Council Assembly.

113.11.14 Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 3th academic year of 113, for reference.

## Chapter 1 General Provisions

Article 1: This constitution is established in accordance with Article 33 of the University Act, Article 26 of the Yuan Ze University Organizational Regulations, and the Regulations on the Establishment and Guidance of Student Autonomous Organizations at Yuan Ze University.

Article 2: The name of this association is the "Yuan Ze University Student Association." It is the highest student autonomous organization representing the students of the university.

Article 3: The purpose of this association is to enhance and implement student autonomy, promote the welfare of its members, pursue progress on campus, maintain harmony and development within the campus, and ensure the rights of its members.

Article 4: The headquarters of this association is located at the main campus of Yuan Ze University.

## Chapter 2 Members

Article 5: Students currently enrolled at the university with student status are automatic members of this association.

Article 6: Members of this association shall have the following basic rights:

1. The right to elect and recall.

2. The right to initiate and referend.

3. The right to participate in various operations and activities organized by the Association.

4. Other rights in accordance with the objectives of the Association.

Article 7: Members of this association shall fulfill the following obligations:

1. Comply with the rules and regulations of the association and the resolutions of the Student Council.

2. Pay membership fees as required.

## Chapter 3 Organization

Article 8: The association establishes the Student Administrative Center, the Student Council, and the Student Review Council.

The Student Administrative Center is the highest administrative body of the association, the Student Council is the highest legislative and deliberative body, and the Student Review Council is the highest review body.

Article 9: The association shall elect students to represent and participate in meetings related to school affairs, subject to the approval of the Student Council. However, when representatives are designated as automatic representatives according to regulations or are elected according to the autonomous regulations of the association, this requirement does not apply.

The method of electing student representatives shall be determined by other autonomous regulations of the association.

## Chapter 4 Student Administrative Center

Article 10: The association shall appoint one President, serving a one-year term with the possibility of reelection for one consecutive term.

The President represents the association externally and provides leadership for the operation of the Student Administrative Center internally.

The association shall appoint one Vice President, serving a one-year term with the possibility of reelection for one consecutive term. The Vice President assists the President in handling the affairs of the association.

The association shall appoint one Secretary-General, serving a one-year term and appoint by the President. The Secretary-General assists in coordinating between the various structures of the association and supports the President and Vice President in matters related to the Student Administrative Center.

Individuals holding positions specified in this article may not concurrently serve as student council members, members of the Student Review Council, or as leaders of other autonomous organizations or clubs at the university.

Article 11: The President has the following powers:

1. The power to promulgate autonomous regulations.

2. The power to veto resolutions of the Student Council.

3. The power to nominate members of the Student Review Council.

4. The power to appoint the heads of the administrative departments of the Student Administrative Center.

5. The authority to preside over meetings of the Student Administrative Center.

6. The authority to execute other tasks as authorized by the constitution or regulations.

Resolutions of the Student Council, except those subject to the President's veto power according to this constitution, shall be announced within ten days from the date of receipt.

Article 12: The powers of the Student Administrative Center are as follows:

1. Execute resolutions of the Student Council.

2. Develop and implement the association's work plan.

3. Handle matters related to the rights and obligations of members.

4. Nominate members of the Election Affairs Committee.

5. Organize and assist in member activities and related events.

6. Propose resolutions to the Student Council.

7. Execute other tasks as authorized by the constitution or regulations.

Article 13: The Student Administrative Center permanently establishes the Secretariat, the Student Rights and Legal Affairs Department, and the Financial Affairs Department. In addition to these permanent departments, other functional departments may be established as needed. The organizational structure of the Student Administrative Center and the responsibilities of each department shall be defined by other autonomous regulations.

Members of the Student Administrative Center may not concurrently serve as Student Council representatives or members of the Student Review Committee.

Article 14: Each department of the Student Administrative Center, except for the Secretariat, where the Secretary-General concurrently handles supervisory duties, shall have one Director or Chairperson, appointed or dismissed by the President. The same procedure applies for appointments or dismissals in the event of a vacancy.

Article 15: In the event of a vacancy in the position of the President, In the event of a vacancy in the Vice President's position, the President shall nominate a candidate within one month, subject to approval by the Student Council, to serve until the end of the original term.

If both the President and Vice President positions are vacant, the Speaker of the Student Council shall act as the President.

If the vacancy exceeds three months, a by-election for the President and Vice President shall be conducted immediately to complete the remainder of the original term.

In the absence of the President due to unforeseen circumstances, the Vice President may act on behalf of the President for a period not exceeding three months.

Article 16: The Student Administrative Center shall convene regular meetings, consisting of the President, Vice President, and the directors of each department.

The President or their designee shall chair the meetings.

The meeting shall only be convened if more than half of the members are present, and resolutions on discussed matters require the agreement of the majority of attendees.

Article 17: The President is responsible for reporting on the operational affairs and work plans of the association at regular meetings of the Student Council.

When the Student Council disagrees with a significant policy of the President, it may pass a resolution requesting the President to make changes. The President may exercise the veto power over resolutions of the Student Council within ten days of the resolution being delivered.

Regarding the autonomous regulations, budget proposals, and resolutions of the Student Council, except for amendments to the organizational regulations, if the President finds the

difficult to implement, the President may exercise the veto power within ten days of the resolution being delivered.

Resolutions of the Student Council vetoed by the President shall be returned to the Student Council for reconsideration. If more than two-thirds of the council members agree to maintain the original resolution, the President shall accept the resolution or resign.

## Chapter 5 Student Council

Article 18 The Student Council is composed of student representatives.

The organizational structure of the Student Council shall be determined by other self-governing regulations.

Article 19 The Student Council consists of fifteen student representatives, elected directly by members in a single electoral district covering the entire campus.

The term of office for student representatives is one year, with the possibility of reelection.

Article 20 The powers of the Student Council are as follows:

1. The authority to approve student autonomous legal proposals and amendments to this constitution.

2. The authority to approve the budget, review the final accounts, and assess the financial condition of the organization.

3. The right to hear reports on the operational activities and work plans of the president.

4. The authority to exercise the consent right of student representatives in the Student Review Council and other meetings related to school affairs.

5. The right to reflect and communicate the opinions of members.

6. The authority to approve proposals put forth by student representatives or the Student Administration Center.

7. The right to request the president to implement resolutions passed by the Student Council.

8. The power to conduct elections and impeach the chairman and vice chairman.

9. The right to bring impeachment charges against the president, vice president, or members of the Student Administration Center for violations of Taiwanese laws, student union regulations, or in cases of negligence.

10. The authority to investigate and propose corrective measures for matters related to the Student Administration Center.

11. Other tasks delegated by regulations.

Impeachment cases specified in the first paragraph, section nine, after being approved by the Student Council, shall be forwarded to the Student Review Council for examination.

Article 21 The Student Council shall have one chairman and one vice chairman, elected by mutual election among the student representatives, serving a term concurrent with that of the representatives.

The chairman is responsible for presiding over the meetings of the Student Council, and the vice chairman assists the chairman in handling business.

In the absence of the chairman, the vice chairman shall perform the duties, and if the vice chairman is absent, a new one shall be elected by the student representatives.

In case the chairman cannot perform the duties for a legitimate reason, the vice chairman may be appointed to exercise the powers.

Article 22 The Student Council consists of regular and ad hoc meetings:

1. Regular meetings shall be held three times per semester within one week after the start of each semester, one month before mid-term exams, and one month before final exams.

2. Ad hoc meetings can be called by the president, or by a petition signed by more than onefourth of all council members.

A meeting may only be convened with the presence of over half of the members, and resolutions shall be passed with the agreement of more than half of the attending members. Resolutions related to the powers specified in Article 20, paragraph 1, section 8, (recall), section 9, (impeachment), and section 10, (disciplinary action), require the approval of over two-thirds of the attending members.

Article 23 The Student Council may establish committees, the organization, rules, meeting times, and venues of which shall be determined by the council members.

Article 24 The Student Council shall establish a Disciplinary Committee to deliberate on disciplinary cases involving student councilors.

The Disciplinary Committee shall consist of five members elected from among the student councilors.

For disciplinary cases involving student councilors, a decision on the validity of the case and the level of punishment requires the agreement of two-thirds of all committee members to pass and must then be submitted to the Student Review Committee for further review.

The Disciplinary Committee may impose the most severe penalty of dismissal on student councilors who violate national laws resulting in a court conviction or commit serious misconduct. A dismissal decision requires the agreement of two-thirds of all Disciplinary Committee members, approval by two-thirds of the Student Council members, and submission to the Student Review Committee for review.

Disciplinary cases involving student councilors must be proposed by a student councilor and approved by the Student Council before being submitted to the Disciplinary Committee.

Matters related to the discipline of student councilors shall be determined by other autonomous regulations .

Article 25 Student representatives may not concurrently hold the following positions： 1.Leadership roles in other autonomous organizations, clubs, or departmental student associations at the university.

2.Membership in the Student Administration Center or the Student Review Council.

Article 26 The Student Council, in the execution of its duties, may request relevant information from the Student Administration Center.

## Chapter 6 Student Review Council

Article 27 The Student Review Committee shall consist of five members, nominated by the President and approved by the Student Council.

The term of office for Student Review Committee members begins on the date of appointment and ends upon dismissal in accordance with student self-governance laws.

Members of the Student Review Committee may not concurrently serve as members of the Student Administrative Center or as student councilors.

Article 28 The powers of the Student Review Council are as follows:

1. Interpretation of the application of this organizational charter and autonomous regulations.

2. Examination of impeachment cases submitted by the Student Council or cases referred by

the Student Council Disciplinary Committee.

3. Assessment of whether the regulations of the organization violate national laws or involve hierarchical conflicts.

4. Evaluation of cases challenging the decisions or measures taken by various organs of the organization.

5. Other matters authorized by regulations or laws.

The organization of the Student Review Council shall be determined by other autonomous regulations.

Article 29 The Student Review Council is a task-oriented agency and shall convene a meeting within one week upon receiving a case.

The council shall exercise its powers through deliberation, and meetings shall be attended by over half of the commissioners.

For the interpretation specified in the first item, examination mentioned in the second item, and assessment specified in the third item of the preceding article, the agreement of over two-thirds of the attending commissioners is required.

For the evaluation specified in the fourth item or other matters authorized by regulations or autonomous regulations, unless otherwise specified in the autonomous regulations, decisions shall require the agreement of over half of the attending commissioners.

Article 30 Impeachment cases against the President, Vice President, or members of the Student Administrative Center shall result in dismissal on the seventh day following the date of approval by the Student Review Committee.

Disciplinary cases involving student councilors shall be executed starting from the day after approval by the Student Review Committee. Dismissal cases involving student councilors shall result in dismissal on the seventh day following the date of approval by the Student Review Committee.

Article 31 In the exercise of its powers, the Student Review Council may request relevant information from the Student Administration Center or the Student Council.

## Chapter 7 Elections and Recalls

Article 32 Elections or recalls shall be conducted through ordinary, equal, direct, and anonymous single-ballot voting.

Article 33 The election of the president and vice president shall be held as a single election district for the entire school, and they shall be directly elected by all members.

In the case of a single candidate for the positions of president and vice president, the election shall adopt a consent-based system, where the candidate with more affirmative votes than negative votes is elected.

In the case of two or more sets of candidates for president and vice president, a relative majority vote shall be used, and the set of candidates with the highest number of votes shall be elected.

Article 34 In the event that no candidate is elected or there is a vacancy in the election of the President, Vice President, or student councilors, a by-election shall be held.

If, after a by-election, no candidate is elected for the President or Vice President, the new Student Council shall elect candidates from among its student councilors before the original term of the Student Council expires. However, if there are fewer than five student councilors, the vacancy shall be considered unfilled, and no by-election shall be held. The provisions of Article 15 shall not apply in this case.

If a vacancy remains after a by-election for student councilors, the total number of seats for that term shall be based on the number of seats filled after the by-election. However, the number of student councilors shall not be fewer than three.

If the vacancies in student councilors reach half of the total number of seats after the by-election, a second by-election shall be held. However, this requirement does not apply if the term is less than three months.

Article 35 The president and vice president may be recalled by the members from their respective election districts.

A recall vote shall be considered passed if the number of votes in favor exceeds the number of votes against.

When a recall proposal passes through the aforementioned process, the recall shall take effect seven days after the announcement of the voting results.

Article 36 The term of office for the president, vice president, and student council members shall begin on July 1 of each year and end on June 30 of the following year. The election of the president, vice president, and student council members shall be completed within thirty days before the expiration of their term each year.

Article 37 Election-related matters shall be handled by the Election Committee.

The Election Committee shall consist of five members, nominated by the President and approved by the Student Council.

Members of the Student Review Committee may not serve as Election Committee members, and Election Committee members may not register as candidates.

Article 38 The regulations for elections and recalls and the organization of the Election Committee shall be determined by other autonomous regulations.

## Chapter 8 Finances

Article 39 The sources of funds for this organization are as follows:

1. Membership dues.

2. Voluntary donations.

3. Various subsidies.

4. Interest from deposits.

5. Other income from business operations.

Article 40 (Deleted).

Article 41 The collection or exemption of membership dues and their amounts shall be determined by the Student Council.

Matters related to the collection of membership dues shall be determined by other autonomous regulations.

## Chapter 9 Supplementary Provisions

Article 42 Amendments to this constitution that conflict with the laws of our country are deemed invalid. Any regulations of this organization's autonomous laws or resolutions of the Student Council and the Student Executive Center that conflict with this constitution are also deemed invalid.

Article 43 The amendment procedure for this constitution is as follows:

If proposed by more than one-fourth of the student council members, with a two-thirds attendance, and approved by two-thirds of the attending student council members, it can be amended.

If decided by the Student Executive Center, it shall be submitted for review by the Student Council. If approved by two-thirds of the attending student council members, with two-thirds of the attending student council members agreeing, it can be amended.

Article 44 This constitution shall take effect from the date of its publication.

The provisions amended on April 6, 2022, shall take effect from the inauguration of the 30th Student Council.

The amendment to Article 19, made on November 30, 2022, shall take effect from the election of the 31st Student Council.

The amendment to Article 37, made on October 15, 2024, shall take effect from the inauguration of the 33rd Student Council.

Article 45 After the constitution is amended through the legal procedure, it shall be announced by the President and implemented, and a copy shall be sent to the Office of Student Affairs at Yuan Ze University for record.

Should there be any controversies or disputes regarding the contents of the above articles, they should always be referred to their Chinese version.
```

# Yuan Ze University Organizational Charter for the Joint-Council of Presidents of Departmental Student Associations

Passed by the 4th Student Affairs Meeting of the academic year on 14 November 2018

Article 1: In order to implement the concept of student autonomy, cultivate students' democratic literacy, promote communication of opinions on campus and enhance the spirit of service, the "Yuan Ze University Organizational Charter of the Joint-council of Presidents of Departmental Student Associations" (hereinafter referred to as the Charter) is formulated.

Article 2: The Joint-council of Presidents of Departmental Student Associations (hereinafter referred to as the Joint-council) is composed of various departmental Student Associations, with the president of each department (or unit at the same level) as the ex-officio representative.

Article 3: The counseling unit of this joint-council is the Extracurricular Affairs Section of the Student Affairs Office, which assists in the election of the president and vice presidents from the Joint-council of Presidents of the Departmental Student Associations.

Article 4: The joint-council shall have a president, two vice-presidents and several officers, who shall be elected at the Departmental Student Association presidents’ meeting. The president is responsible for convening and presiding over at least two departmental student association presidents’ meetings each semester, as well as cadre meetings during the semester.

Article 5: The responsibilities of this joint-council are as follows:

1. Assist in the student and extracurricular activities organized by the University and various departmental student associations.

2. Handle and coordinate common affairs among various of the departmental student associations, and strive for relevant rights and interests.

3. Promote friendships and exchange communication among various departmental student associations.

4. Attend on-campus meetings related to student rights and handle the related activities on its behalf if the Student Association cannot be re-elected for some reasons.

Article 6: This charter shall come into effect after being approved by the Executive Meeting of the Student Affairs Office, and the same situations should be applied when revised.

Should there be any controversies or disputes regarding the contents of the above articles, they should always be referred to their Chinese version.
```

# Guidelines for the Installation and Management of Security Surveillance Video Systems in Yuan Ze University Student Dormitories

06.06.2019 Ratified in the 9th Student Affair Meeting of academic year 2018

## Article1

In order to maintain the safety of student dormitories at Yuan Ze University, protect the rights of the dormitory students and prevent the improper use of related information, the "Guidelines for the Installation and Management of Security Surveillance Video Systems in Yuan Ze University Student Dormitories" is hereby established. Hereinafter referred to as “Guidelines”.

## Article2

The Surveillance Video Systems (SVS) and surrounding related facilities in the student dormitories are installed in public areas which is necessary for security, such as underground parking lots, dormitory exits, monitoring and management rooms, corridors, elevators. The Students Housing Service Section (SHSS) of the Student Affairs Office (SAO) is responsible for managing it.

## Article3

In order to maintain the safety and normal operation on SVS data, the counselors of SHSS should conduct daily inspections, report malfunctions and record them in the "Dormitory Counselors Duty Log". Counselors and System Administrators should be familiar with the operations of the SVS system and note the following points:

(1) When there is a change in personnel, related equipments and SVS data should be handed over to the person in charge. Former personnel have a duty of confidentiality with respect to SVA data during their tenure.

(2) SVS equipments should be continuously operated without unreasonable interruption. The video recording should be kept for at least ten days, and the recorded image should be kept for at least six months.

## Article4

The procedures of applying for reviewing and copying SVS data are as follows:

(1) Applicants are limited to the parties involved in the videos. They have to fill in a form of "Application Form for Review to Security Surveillance Video Data in Student Dormitories of Yuan Ze University" (as attached) within three days of the accident, explaining the reason for review and pointing out the required location and timeframe. After being approved by the Dean of SHSS, the Counselors/School Security Personnel/ System Administrators will accompany with the applicants during the reviewing/copying process.

(2) In case of loss or damage on official equipments or personal items, for investigating

campus security incidents, Public Security Agencies need SVA data as evidences for the investigation of civil and criminal cases or other disputes, SVS data reviewing can be applied for.

(3) For general application, the working hours are from 8:30am to 5:00pm, Monday to Friday.   
Emergency cases can be served at any time.

## Article5

Actions related to this Guidelines should comply with the regulations of "Personal Data Protection and Management Guidelines" of YZU, and adhere to the "Personal Data Protection Act" and other relevant laws and regulations. If any improper use is discovered, the applicants is liable to the laws.

## Article6

This Guidelines is approved during the SAO meeting, and promulgated for implementation after being approved by the Dean of SAO. The same procedures for amendments.
```

# Review Rules for Student Academic Reward and Versatility Reward College of Engineering, Yuan Ze University

Approved by the 4th College Affairs Meeting in the 1998 academic year on January 6, 1999   
Amended by the 5th College Affairs Meeting in the 1998 academic year on April 14, 1999   
Amended by the 6th College Affairs Meeting in the 1998 academic year on May 20, 1999   
Amended by the 2nd College Affairs Meeting in the 2000 academic year on November 8th, 2000   
Amended by the 5th College Affairs Meeting in the 2001 academic year on April 10th, 2002   
Amended by the 6th College Affairs Meeting in the 2004 academic year on June 22, 2005   
Amended by the 5th College Affairs Meeting in the 2017 academic year on April 11, 2018   
Verified by the 5th Student Affairs Meeting in the 2017 academic year on May 10, 2018   
Amended by the 4th College Affairs Meeting in the 2018 academic year on May 21, 2019   
Verified by the 1st Student Affairs Meeting in the 2019 academic year on October 2, 2019   
Verified by the 3th Student Affairs Meeting in the 2021 academic year on April 27, 2022

Article 1 To encourage students with outstanding academic achievements and versatility in each department, the College of Engineering (hereinafter referred to as “this College”) established the review guidelines according to the reward instructions issued by this university.

Article 2 Students from all departments of this College who meet the following requirements are eligible to apply for the Academic Awards:

1. Academic Gold Award: Students who have received first place in a national academic competition or first/second/third place or an award in an international academic competition. Undergraduate or graduate students who have their study or research results published or accepted for publication by reputable domestic or foreign journals (Category A journals). A paper can only be used once for this application. Only one author of the paper can file an application; for applications of two or more authors, the advisors must provide an explanation in the application form.

2. Academic Silver Award: Students who have received first/second/third place in intramural and extramural academic competitions. Undergraduate or graduate students who have their study or research results published or accepted for publication by reputable domestic or foreign journals (Category B journals). A paper can only be used once for this application. Only one author of the paper can file an application; for applications of two or more authors, the advisors must provide an explanation in the application form.

3. Academic Achievement Award: Students who have received two Academic Silver Awards or one Academic Gold Award and again qualify for the Academic Gold Award in the year of application.

Article 3 Students from all departments of this College who meet the following requirements are eligible to apply for the Versatility Awards:

1. Versatility Gold Award: Students who have passed the National Civil Service Senior Examination (or examinations of an equivalent level), received a National Technician Skills Class A Certification, or obtained an excellent English proficiency result (refer to the English Proficiency Tests and CEF Table for Award/Medal Application issued by this university).

2. Versatility Silver Award: Students who have passed the National Civil Service Junior Examination (or examinations of an equivalent level), received a National Technician Skills Class B Certification, or obtained an excellent English proficiency result (refer to the English Proficiency Tests and CEF Table for Award/Medal Application issued by this university).

3. Versatility Achievement Award: Students who have received two Versatility Silver Awards or one Versatility Gold Award and again qualify for the Versatility Gold Award in the year of application.

Article 4 Students who are qualified to apply can submit the following supporting documents provided by themselves or relevant units: study or research results, photocopies of papers published or accepted by domestic or foreign journals, competition results or awards of academic competitions, transcripts of the National Examinations, or Technician Skill Certifications. The application is to be submitted to the department to which the applicant belongs. Awardee selection is to be conducted by the Engineering College Affairs Meeting. Following result approval by the Student Affairs Meeting, the Award winners are to be announced by the Office of Student Affairs.

Article 5 An examination or certification result can only be used to apply for either the Gold or Silver Award. Only one Award is to be awarded for an application with multiple results submitted. The Achievement Awards are limited to the graduates of the current year.

Article 6 Award winners who have provided counterfactuals are to be disqualified through the same review procedures.

Article 7 The award winning record is to be registered in the award winner’s Five Ways of Life record by the Office of Student Affairs.

Article 8 The guidelines and amendments herein are approved by the College Affairs Meeting and implemented following verification by the Student Affairs Meeting.
```

## Implementation Regulations for the Happy Learning Camp Project of the Yuan Ze University Diverse Learning Passport

Proposal Presented at the 5th Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 109th Academic Year on December 3, 109

Article 1: In order to improve care and guidance for economically disadvantaged students, these implementation regulations are established in accordance with the provisions of the "Implementation Measures for the Diverse Learning Passport" (hereinafter referred to as the implementation measures).

## Article 2: Purpose of the Activities

Through training in the form of club-like organizations, the project aims to carry out service programs, course learning, book clubs, and other activities to assist students in planning learning strategies, enhancing their motivation and effectiveness in learning, cultivating enthusiasm for community service, and serving society with gratitude and care.

## Article 3: Target Participants

(1) Students who meet the requirements stated in Article 3 of the implementation measures.

(2) Participants will be recruited by the Student Affairs Office's Life Guidance Division (hereinafter referred to as the Life Guidance Division) for the project activities.

(3) Students with poor attitudes toward learning and service, despite counseling, those who unreasonably fail to participate in group activities or submit reflections will have their participation eligibility canceled.

## Article 4: Implementation Methods

(1) Each group's learning activities, such as book clubs and course learning, will be conducted for 4 hours per month.

(2) Each individual should engage in personal learning activities for 4 hours per month.

(3) Each month, participants are required to dedicate 10 hours to group service and care activities (including writing one reflection of 300 words).

(4) Participants should attend group learning courses for 4 hours per month (including writing one reflection of 300 words).

(5) Participants attending all scheduled monthly learning activities and totaling at least 22 hours will receive an additional 3 hours of attendance credit.

(6) Workshops for team training, off-campus community service activities, and the final results presentation will be conducted during each semester. Outstanding students showing enthusiasm for service will be rewarded to enhance team cohesion.

(7) Participants must fill out activity record forms and have them signed by the responsible personnel at the end of each activity. Relevant proof of participation should be retained.

(8) After activity verification and approval, the recorded hours will be processed in accordance with the implementation measures for the Diverse Learning Passport.

## Article 5: Counseling Mechanism

(1) The Life Guidance Division will hold regular monthly meetings with participants to provide guidance and support for the activities' execution and effectiveness.

(2) A community support system will be established to continuously monitor students' learning progress and provide timely assistance in academic counseling, career exploration, financial aid, family or psychological counseling, and appropriate referrals to relevant professional units for consultations.

## Article 6: These implementation regulations will be put into effect after being approved by the Student Affairs Office Meeting and will be subject to revision if necessary.
```

## Yuan Ze University Multifaceted Learning Passport Career Special Teams Project Activity Implementation Regulations

Passed during the 5th Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 109th Academic Year on December 3, 2010   
Amended during the 2nd Student Affairs Office Meeting of the 112th Academic Year on November 2, 2023

Article 1: In order to enhance the care and counseling for economically disadvantaged students, these implementation regulations are established in accordance with Article 4 of the "Implementation Regulations for Yuan Ze University Multifaceted Learning Passport" (hereinafter referred to as "Implementation Regulations").

Article 2: Purpose of Activities: To cultivate students' career employability, including organizational management, business writing, event planning, teamwork, critical thinking and problem-solving, workplace etiquette, stage charisma, self-marketing skills, and to develop a globally oriented perspective.

## Article 3: Application Method:

1. The Student Affairs Office Counseling and Career Development Division (hereinafter referred to as the "Counseling and Career Division") recruits project activity participants.

2. All students eligible under Article 3 of the Implementation Regulations may apply for project activities. However, they must undergo selection and training assessments by the organizing unit. Registered activity hours shall be handled according to the regulations of the Yuan Ze University Multifaceted Learning Passport Implementation Regulations.

3. If a student exhibits poor attendance service attitude, fails to adhere to team agreements, or does not achieve half of the monthly career activity hours, despite being counseled twice by the instructor for improvement, their participation eligibility will be revoked.

## Article 4: Implementation Methods:

1. Conduct learning growth camps, Tri-Arrow workshops, and related training seminars every semester.

2. Hold team leader meetings once every 2 weeks.

3. Participate in life/career activities organized by the Counseling and Career Division, register via the portal activity page, and actively assist in organizing, recruiting, interview editing, planning, marketing, web management, and administrative assistance.

4. Document activities with activity proposals, meeting records, and review recommendations.

5. Attend a minimum of 20 hours of duty per month. Students recommended by the organizing teacher for outstanding performance will receive an additional 3 hours of attendance.

6. Submit a 500-word "Career Information Thumbs Up" activity sharing article monthly.

7. Upon completion of activities, the organizing teacher will complete online certification and retain related proof of participation. Team members must apply for registration according to the regulations and details of the Yuan Ze University Multifaceted Learning Passport.

8. Conduct appreciation ceremonies based on the actual execution of various activities to enhance the honor and sense of mission of students.

Article 5: Counseling Mechanism:

1. The Counseling and Career Division establishes Line groups to care for student interaction status at any time, timely assisting with individual student needs such as academic counseling, life/career exploration, financial assistance, family issues, or psychological counseling. After listening, understanding, and caring, relevant professional units will be referred for counseling based on categories.

2. Upon graduation, depending on their performance, students may receive assistance in writing complete resumes or recommendation letters to improve the career counseling mechanism.

Article 6: These implementation regulations shall be implemented upon approval by the Student Affairs Office Meeting and amended accordingly.

The English version is provided for reference purposes only. In the event of any discrepancies between the English and Chinese versions, the Chinese version shall prevail
```

# Yuan Ze University Academic Award and Versatility Award Review Rules for Students from the College of Electrical and Communication Engineering

Oct.20.2021, Approved by the 2nd college affairs meeting of the 110 Academic Year Apr.27.2022, Approved by the 3rd student affairs meeting of the 110 Academic Year

Article 1 In order to encourage students of the College of Electrical and Communication (hereinafter referred to as “the College”) to have excellent and outstanding academic performance during their studies, the College has formulated these regulations in accordance with the Student Award Regulations of the University.

Article 2 Students who fulfill the following requirements are eligible to apply for academic or multi-skill awards:

1. Academic Gold Quality Award: Those who have won the first place in a national academic competition, the first three places in an international academic competition, or honors in an academic competition, and those in undergraduate or graduate program whose studies or research results have been published in prestigious journals at home and abroad, and the journals are an A-grade journal of the College.

2. Academic Silver Quality Award: Those who are the top three winners of internal and external academic competitions, and those in undergraduate or graduate program whose studies or research results have been published in prestigious journals at home and abroad, and the journals are an B-grade journal of the College.

3. Academic Achievement Award: Those who have received two Academic Silver Quality Awards or one Academic Gold Quality Award and are eligible to apply for the Academic Gold Quality Award again.

4. Multi-Skills Gold Quality Award: Those who have passed the national senior examination (including equivalent examinations), the college-recognized Grade A national technician skills test or language test with outstanding results (according to Student Award Regulations of Yuan Ze University).

5. Multi-Skills Silver Quality Award: Those who have passed the national junior examination (including equivalent examinations), the college-recognized Grade B national technician skills test or language test with outstanding results (according to Student Award Regulations of Yuan Ze University).

6. Multi-skill Achievement Award: Those who have won the Multi-Skill Silver Quality Award twice or the Multi-Skill Gold Quality Award once and are eligible to apply for the Multi-Skill Gold Award again.

Article 3 Students who are eligible for this award may apply to the department (group, program) or to a unit at the same level for recommendation by themselves or by the relevant unit based on relevant information, such as study or research results, copies of papers from famous domestic and foreign journals, and results or awards won in academic competitions. The application will be reviewed at the College meeting and then sent to the student affairs meeting of the Office of Student Affairs for re-examination.

Article 4 Matters not covered in these rules shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Student Award Regulations of the University.

Article 5 These rules will be approved by the college affairs meeting and submitted to the student affairs meeting for approval before implementation.

In case of any discrepancy between the Chinese and English versions, the Chinese version shall prevail.
```

# Implementation Points of Yuan Ze University to Promote the Safety and Service of Students' Off-campus Rental House

2021.12.02: Adopted during the 3rd Student Affairs Meeting of the Year 2021

I. In order to deepen the implementation of the safety and service work of the offcampus residence for students at the University, Yuan Ze University has formulated the "Implementation Points of Yuan Ze University to Promote the Safety and Service of Students' Off-Campus Rental House" (hereinafter referred to as these Points), in accordance with the Ministry of Education's guidelines for promoting the safety and service work of college students' off-campus rental house.

II. The implementation of important items:

(1) Holding meetings of the work promotion group:

The meeting shall be held at least once in each academic year, chaired by the Dean of Studies, and composed of 7 to 11 members, including the Director of the Military Training Office, the head of the Life Counseling Section of the Academic Affairs Office, teachers (instructors), and representatives of the resident students. The meeting may also invite representatives of the police, fire department, and landlords of the district, as appropriate, to discuss the objectives, priorities, and implementation of off-campus housing service for students in the academic year. The aim is to enhance the safety of off-campus accommodation and protect students' rental rights.

(2) Conducting safety self-inspection of students' off-campus accommodation: Implement the "safety self-inspection of the residence" every semester and take appropriate measures according to the results of the self-evaluation of the students, "need to track and improve the guidance". Those who have safety concerns will be sent to conduct care visits.

(3) Conducting safety care visits at students' off-campus accommodation: Implement the "Stay Safety Care Visit" to proactively care for students residing offcampus. All safety concerns regarding student off-campus accommodation should be addressed by visiting the site to check for adverse conditions. The student (parents) and the landlord should be informed of any necessary improvements, and records should be maintained to track progress. If the situation does not improve after review, the student (parents) should be notified again, with a recommendation to move out as soon as possible.

(4) Conducting multiple educational advocacy activities:

1. Accommodation Safety Lectures: The number of accommodation safety lectures will vary each semester to enhance students' knowledge of off-campus

accommodation safety. 2

2. Rental Fair: It will be held once every academic year, providing a platform for three-way communication among students, landlords, and schools to enhance and improve students' rental rights and related knowledge.

3. Landlord seminars: Seminars will be held once every academic year, inviting landlords to provide legal knowledge on fire safety, fire escape, prevention of carbon monoxide poisoning, lease contracts of rented premises, and promoting the school's rental services and safety regulations.

(5) Establishment of off-campus House-rental Network:

Establish the "Off-campus House-rental Network" (https://house.nfu.edu.tw/YZU), attached to the Ministry of Education's "Cloud House Rental Life Network" platform system, to provide information for students and their parents who are renting a house off-campus. The residence information must be verified by checking the owner's identity, building title certificate or tax bill, the lessor's letter of authorization for the management of the rental house, and the verification of the Ministry of Education's care visit security program before logging in.

(6) Set up a consultation window to provide relocation-related services: Set up a relocation-related consultation hotline (03-4638800 ext. 2245) to provide students with consultation regarding relocation and lease disputes coordination services. When students have lease disputes, assistance will be provided in referring relevant units for appeals, mediation, or adjustments. Additionally, depending on the severity of the incident, the Ministry of Education's campus safety and disaster prevention and rescue notification center will be notified accordingly.

III. The personal data collected, processed, or used in this article shall obtain the consent of the parties involved (students, lease lessors) and be recorded for reference in accordance with the relevant provisions of the Personal Data Protection Law.

IV. These points shall be implemented after the approval of the Office of Academic Affairs at its executive meeting, and the same shall apply when amended.
```

# Regulations for Students with Excellent Academic Performance and Skills Award College of Informatics, Yuan Ze University

December 2, 2021 Amended by the 2nd College Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2021-22   
April 27, 2022 Approved by the 3rd university affair meeting of academic year 2021-22

Article 1 Purpose: The Regulations for Students with Excellent Academic Performance and Skills Award was formulated in order to recognize students’ excellent performance in academic studies and related fields during their study at the College of Informatics (hereafter referred to as the College).

Article 2 Eligibility: Awardees must meet the following requirements:

(1) The Gold Academic Medal: This award is given to undergraduate or master’s degree students who have won the top three in any international competition or the best in a national competition. The award is also offered to students whose academic papers have been accepted by any A level academic journals ranked by the College. Each paper can only apply once for any award from the College.

(2) The Silver Academic Medal: The award is given to undergraduate or master’s degree students whose academic papers have been accepted by any B level academic journals ranked by the College. Each paper can only apply once for any award from the College.

(3) The Academic Achievement Award: The award is given to students who have won two silver academic medals or one gold academic medal. The awardees must meet the qualification for applying for another gold academic medal.

(4) The Gold Medal for Professional Skills: This award is given to students who have passed a national examination (or equivalent examination) and are recognized by the College as qualified as a Class A technician. Students who have excellent scores in language proficiency tests could also apply for the award (in accordance with the Reward Details for Students at Yuan Ze University).

(5) The Silver Medal for Professional Skills: This award is given to students who have passed a national examination (or equivalent examination) and are recognized by the College as qualified as a Class B technician. Students who have excellent scores in language proficiency tests could also apply for the award (in accordance with the Reward Details for Students at Yuan Ze University).

(6) The Achievement Award for Professional Skills: The award is given to students who have won two silver medals or one gold medal in this category. The awardees must meet the qualification for applying for another gold academic medal.

Article 3 Application Procedures: Qualified applicants can apply by themselves or be recommended by their department. Documents to be submitted include the study or research results, a copy of the published paper, a certificate of winning competition, or data about the prize. The applicants must provide these documents for obtaining the recommendation from the department. Applications will be reviewed by the College. The list of awardees will be announced after the Student Affair Instructing Committee meeting ratify the result.

Article 4 For matters not listed here, please refer to the Reward Details for Students at Yuan Ze University.

Article 5 This Regulations was approved at the Meeting of Administrative Executives in the College and Student Affair Instructing Committee of Yuan Ze University before implementation. All amendments shall follow the same procedures.
```

# Academic Award and Diverse Skills Award Review Regulations College of Management, Yuan Ze University

Approved in the 3rd College Affairs Meeting of the 110th academic year on December 15, 110 Ratified in the 3rd Student Affairs Meeting of the 110th academic year on April 27, 111 Please see the Chinese version for the detailed history of regulation revision.

## Article 1:

To encourage the students of the College of Management (hereinafter referred to as "the College") to excel in academic and diverse skills during their enrollment, these review regulations are established in accordance with the university's Student Reward Methods.

## Article 2:

Students of the College are eligible to apply for the Academic Award if they meet the following conditions:

1. Gold Academic Award: First place in national academic competitions, top three in international academic competitions, special honors in academic competitions, or undergraduate and master's students whose learning or research results have been published in well-known journals domestically or internationally and are classified as level I or II by the College.

2. Silver Academic Award: Top three in academic competitions organized by internal or external institutions, or undergraduate and master's students whose learning or research results have been published in well-known journals domestically or internationally and are classified as level III by the College.

3. Academic Achievement Award: Those who have received two Silver Academic Awards or one Gold Academic Award and again meet the qualifications for the Gold Award.

## Article 3:

Students of the College are eligible to apply for the Diverse Skills Award if they meet the following conditions:

1. Gold Diverse Skills Award: Passed national higher examinations (including equivalent exams), A-level national technical certification, or outstanding language test scores recognized by the College (in accordance with the university's Student Reward Methods).

2. Silver Diverse Skills Award: Passed national general examinations (including equivalent exams), B-level national technical certification, or outstanding language test scores recognized by the College (in accordance with the university's Student Reward Methods).

3. Diverse Skills Achievement Award: Those who have received two Silver Diverse Skills Awards or one Gold Diverse Skills Award and again meet the qualifications for the Gold Award.

## Article 4:

Students eligible for these awards may apply for program recommendation by themselves or through relevant units by providing relevant documents such as learning or research results, photocopies of papers published in well-known domestic or international journals, academic competition results or awards, and national examination or certification scores. After selection by the College, the results will be announced following approval by the Student Affairs Meeting of the Office of Student Affairs.

## Article 5:

Matters not covered in these regulations shall be handled in accordance with the university's Student Reward Methods.

## Article 6:

These regulations are implemented after approval by the College Affairs Meeting and ratification by the Student Affairs Meeting, and the same applies to any amendments.
```

# Student Academic Award and Multi-Skills Award Review Regulations, College of Humanities and Social Sciences, Yuan Ze University

Amended by the 3rd Student Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2021, on April 27, 2022

Article 1 The College of Humanities and Social Sciences (hereinafter referred to as “the College”) has formulated these regulations in accordance with the Student Award Scheme of the College in order to encourage students who present outstanding academic and multi-skill achievements during their study in the College.

Article 2 Students who fulfill the following requirements are eligible to apply for the Academic or Multi-Skills Award:

1. Gold Medal in Academics: Those who have won the top three places in international academic competitions, the first place in national academic competitions, or honors. Undergraduate and master's students whose studies or research results have been published or accepted in prestigious domestic and international journals and A-ranked journals belonging to the College can apply for the same paper only once.

2. Silver Medal in Academics: Students who have won the top three prizes in internal and external academic competitions. Undergraduate and master's degree students whose studies or research results have been published or accepted in famous domestic and foreign journals and B-level journals belonging to the College can apply for the same paper only once.

3. Academic Achievement Award: Students who have received two Silver Medals or one Gold Medal in Academics are eligible to apply for the Gold Medal in Academics again.

4. Multi-Skills Gold Award: Those who have passed the national higher education exams (including equivalent exams), the national technician's skills test or language test recognized by the colleges and universities with outstanding results (refer to the comparison table between the English test and the CEF of Yuan Ze University's award application categories).

5. Multi-skills Silver Award: Those who have passed the national general examination (including equivalent examination), and those who have excelled in Grade B national technician skills test or language test as recognized by the colleges and universities (refer to YUCC awards to apply for various English tests and CEF comparison forms).

6. Multi-Skills Achievement Award: Students who have received the Multi-Skills Silver Award twice or the Multi-Skills Gold Award once are eligible to apply for the Multi-Skills Gold Award again.

Article 3 Students who meet the application requirements may apply to their respective departments, classes, or units at the same level for recommendation by themselves or the relevant organizations with relevant information such as study or research results, academic competition results, awards, etc. After a preliminary examination by the College, the application will be submitted to the Student Affairs Council for review and approval and then announced.

Article 4 After the preliminary examination, the student affairs meeting will review and approve the application and announce the awards.

Article 5 This is designed to provide students an opportunity to learn and learn from each other.

 The English translation is for reference only. In case of any discrepancy between Chinese version and English version, the Chinese version shall prevail.
```

# Yuan Ze University Sports Award Review Regulations

Passed at the 8th Physical Education Room Affairs Meeting for the 2016 academic year on April 21, 2017. Verified at the 3rd Student Affairs Meeting for the 2016 academic year on May 10, 2017. Revised at the 3rd Physical Education Room Affairs Meeting for the 2021 academic year on November 24, 2021. Verified at the 3rd Student Affairs Meeting for the 2021 academic year on April 27, 2022.

Article 1: These regulations are formulated in accordance with the Student Awards Regulations of Yuan Ze University to encourage students to achieve outstanding performance in sports during their time at the university. Hereinafter referred to as these regulations.

Article 2: Students meeting the following conditions may apply:

Achievement Award: Eligible for recent graduates who have received the Silver Award twice or the Gold Award once and meet the Gold Award application criteria again.

Gold Award:

(1) Those who have achieved the top three positions or received special honors in international sports competitions representing the university.

(2) Those who have achieved the top three positions or received special honors in nationally renowned sports competitions representing the university.

(3) Record holders in innovative national sports competitions.

Silver Award:

(1) Those who have achieved fourth to eighth place in nationally recognized sports competitions representing the university.

(2) Those who have won championships or received special honors in regional sports competitions representing the university.

(3) Record holders in innovative university sports.

Article 3: Applicants meeting the qualifications for each award category may submit an application form and proof of achievements to the Physical Education Room. After approval by the Physical Education Room Affairs Meeting, the application will be forwarded to the Student Affairs Meeting for further review.

Article 4: The application period for these awards will be announced by the Student Affairs Office.   
Applicants should keep relevant records and proofs properly during normal times.

Article 5: Matters not covered in these regulations will be handled in accordance with the Student Awards Regulations of Yuan Ze University.

Article 6: These regulations, once approved by the Physical Education Room Affairs Meeting and verified by the Student Affairs Meeting, will be implemented. Amendments shall follow the same process.
```

# Points for the establishment of the Indigenous Student Resource Center at Yuan Ze University

Approved at the 7th Administrative Meeting of the 111th Academic Year on October 26, 111   
Amended and passed in the 14th Administrative Meeting of the 112th Academic Year on March 13, 113   
Amended and passed in the 22nd Administrative Meeting of the 112th Academic Year on July 10, 113

Article 1:Yuan Ze University, hereinafter referred to as "the university," aims to develop a campus characterized by multiculturalism and integrate internal and external resources. In order to provide guidance and enhance the learning effectiveness of indigenous students, the Indigenous Student Resource Center (hereinafter referred to as "the Center") is established in accordance with the Indigenous Education Act and Article 7 of the university's organizational regulations, under the Student Affairs Office.

Article 2:The primary missions of the Center are as follows:

1. To coordinate and integrate the University's cross-departmental Indigenous student affairs and resources.

2. To monitor and support the academic performance of Indigenous students at the University.

3. To care for and assist Indigenous students in adapting to campus life.

4. To promote and cultivate an Indigenous cultural environment, creating a diverse and distinctive campus character.

Article 3:The Center shall have one Director, who concurrently serves as the Dean of Student Affairs, overseeing the Center's operations. The Center may also have several staff members to assist with various programs and activities, who will be appointed from the University's existing personnel or hired on a contractual basis.

Article 4:The Center shall establish a Advisory Committee to provide consultation and evaluation on the Center's operations and development. The Committee shall meet at least once per academic year, with additional meetings called as necessary. The Advisory Committee shall consist of five to seven members, appointed by the University President upon the Center's recommendation each academic year. The term of appointment is one year, and members may be reappointed upon the expiration of their term. The composition of the Advisory Committee is as follows:

1. Ex-officio member: The Director of the Center.

2. Appointed members: External professionals, representatives of Indigenous students, or University faculty and staff with Indigenous

backgrounds.

3. Indigenous members must constitute at least one-third of the total number of committee members.

Article 5:These guidelines shall be implemented following approval by the Administrative Council, and the same applies to any amendments.
```
